The family owned and operated hotel features world-class design with locally inspired dining and premier event space.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=435360\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-435360\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-435360\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/11/thelakehousecanandaigua_studiotack_13-810x456.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"456\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/11/thelakehousecanandaigua_studiotack_13-810x456.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/11/thelakehousecanandaigua_studiotack_13-800x450.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/11/thelakehousecanandaigua_studiotack_13-768x432.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/11/thelakehousecanandaigua_studiotack_13-600x337.jpg 600w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/11/thelakehousecanandaigua_studiotack_13.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p>Envisioned by The Brooklyn Company, led by brother-sister developer Bill Caleo, designer Lyndsay Caleo Karol and her artist husband Fitzhugh Karol, the development of the hotel features residentially-inspired spaces focused on travelers seeking an active wellness retreat.</p>\n<p>The property includes 125-guest rooms and suites with a timber-frame event barn, pool, year-round hot tub, spa, wellness center and boardwalk. Attached is signature restaurant Rose Tavern featuring vaulted ceilings centered around a wood fire hearth.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=435359\" rel=\"attachment /></a></p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p>Located on a corner lot in Prairie Village, Kansas, the Homestead Residence is a <a href=\"https://kemstudio.com/projects/homestead-residence/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">project</a> by <a href=\"https://kemstudio.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">KEM STUDIO</a> that gives nod to mid-century modern design and the original home that once stood there. A low slung hipped roof connects the main house structures and the garage, while allowing space for a covered outdoor room for the family to enjoy, as well access to the backyard.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=436563\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-436563\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-436563\" 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Homestead-Residence-Kansas-KEM-Studio-2-768x512.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Homestead-Residence-Kansas-KEM-Studio-2.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p>The front facade combines a tan brick with stained cedar, along with smaller elements of white stucco and exposed concrete, which present a warm and inviting presence in a mostly traditional neighborhood.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=436564\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-436564\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p>The front facade pivots to an angle before rotating again to rest of the structure with an open-air space in between that houses the family&#8217;s outdoor living room.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=436565\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-436565\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large Artists","link":"https://design-milk.com/?p=436228","description":"\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/venus-the-cat-collaborates-with-uk-street-artists/venus-and-the-cat-tools-of-the-trade/\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Venus-and-the-cat-tools-of-the-trade-e1607379257524-810x694.jpg\" alt=\"Venus &#038; the Cat Collaborates With UK Street Artists\" /></a></p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p><a href=\"https://shop.design-milk.com/collections/venus-the-cat\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"exclude\">Venus &#38; the Cat</a>, makers of bespoke urban homeware, collaborates with standout talent from the UK’s street art scene. The brand crafts exclusive limited-edition fine bone china that captures the heart of British street art and allows artists to create work that won’t be covered or washed away. Blending machine and century-old hand-crafting techniques, each piece passes through over 20 pairs of skilled hands during its creation.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=436230\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-436230\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-436230\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Venus-and-the-cat-tools-of-the-trade-2-810x810.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"810\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Venus-and-the-cat-tools-of-the-trade-2-810x810.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Venus-and-the-cat-tools-of-the-trade-2-800x800.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Venus-and-the-cat-tools-of-the-trade-2-100x100.jpg 100w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Venus-and-the-cat-tools-of-the-trade-2-768x768.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Venus-and-the-cat-tools-of-the-trade-2-300x300.jpg 300w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Venus-and-the-cat-tools-of-the-trade-2.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p><a href=\"https://shop.design-milk.com/collections/venus-the-cat/products/katrina-russell-adams-pot\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"exclude\">The Tools of the Trade Planter</a> is an exclusively commissioned work by renowned visual artist Katrina Russell-Adams. Only 50 of these indoor plant pots were made. Katrina Russell-Adams&#8217; art is informed by the joyful clash of diversity, shapes, the people and places around her. Her eye-catching, bold work has adorned the streets and galleries of London. For her Venus &#38; the Cat collab, she used the ceramic craftsmanship process to inform the shapes and themes of her work.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=436231\" href=\"https://design-milk.com/humans-since-1982-launch-the-kinetic-clockclock-9/clockclock_9_humans_photo_tim_meier_featured-image/\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img /></a></p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p><a href=\"https://www.humanssince1982.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Humans since 1982</a>, a.k.a. Bastian Bischoff and Per Emanuelsson, have added to their ongoing project – <a href=\"http://clockclock.com\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">ClockClock</a> – with <a href=\"https://clockclock.com/collections/clockclock-9\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">ClockClock 9</a>. Parts art, design and <a href=\"https://shop.design-milk.com/collections/tech-1\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"exclude\">technology</a>, the kinetic piece is comprised of nine pairs of clock hands mounted to a mineral composite housing. As the hands move through their choreography, you&#8217;ll notice they do so both independently and in formation as they continuously alternate between abstract and synchronized movements.</p>\n<p><iframe src=\"https://player.vimeo.com/video/480867491?byline=0&#38;portrait=0\" width=\"810\" height=\"456\" frameborder=\"0\" allowfullscreen=\"allowfullscreen\"></iframe></p>\n<div id=\"attachment_436019\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\"><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=436019\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-436019\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"size-large wp-image-436019\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/ClockClock_9_Humans_Photo_Tim_Meier_1-810x1215.jpg\" alt=\"modern clock\" width=\"810\" height=\"1215\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/ClockClock_9_Humans_Photo_Tim_Meier_1-810x1215.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/ClockClock_9_Humans_Photo_Tim_Meier_1-800x1200.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/ClockClock_9_Humans_Photo_Tim_Meier_1-768x1152.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/ClockClock_9_Humans_Photo_Tim_Meier_1-1024x1536.jpg 1024w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/ClockClock_9_Humans_Photo_Tim_Meier_1.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a><p class=\"wp-caption-text\">Photo: Tim Meier</p></div>\n<p>ClockClock 9 is currently available for pre-order in a limited edition of 50 pieces. Humans since 1982&#8217;s most affordable kinetic work to date, each one is carefully assembled in their Stockholm, Sweden studio before being signed and numbered. Upon delivery it will be packaged with a certificate of authenticity, an operator&#8217;s manual, a hanging bracket and art handling gloves. ClockClock 9 will be delivered during the first quarter of 2021.</p>\n<div id=\"attachment_436020\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\"><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=436020\" Time","link":"https://design-milk.com/?p=436357","description":"\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/vestre-is-helping-save-the-oceans-one-bench-at-a-time/vestre-coast-bench-featured-image/\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Vestre-Coast-Bench-Featured-Image-810x532.png\" alt=\"Vestre Is Helping Save the Oceans, One Bench at a Time\" /></a></p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p>Manufacturer of urban <a href=\"https://shop.design-milk.com/collections/furnishings\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"exclude\">furniture</a>, <a href=\"https://vestre.com/us/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Vestre</a>, and ocean impact startup <a href=\"https://www.ogoori.eco/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Oogori</a> have joined forces to create the <a href=\"https://vestre.com/us/news/the-world-s-first-bench-made-from-ownerless-marine-plastic\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Coast bench</a>. Made entirely from ownerless marine plastics gathered on the beaches of Norway and the first of its kind, Coast was designed by Allan Hagerup to withstand outdoor marine environments. But it&#8217;s the plastic material itself that&#8217;s guided the design process.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=436361\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-436361\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-436361\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Vestre-Coast-Bench-1-810x1201.png\" alt=\"bench on beach\" width=\"810\" height=\"1201\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Vestre-Coast-Bench-1-810x1201.png 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Vestre-Coast-Bench-1-800x1186.png 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Vestre-Coast-Bench-1-768x1139.png 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Vestre-Coast-Bench-1-1036x1536.png 1036w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Vestre-Coast-Bench-1.png 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<blockquote><p>Designing a bench using plastic gathered from beaches by volunteers is an inspiring and passionate task. So it feels great to have created the very first bench in this material for Vestre, and to contribute to sustainable development with a product that will be accessible to everyone.</p></blockquote>\n<p><em>-Allan Hagerup</em></p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=436362\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-436362\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-436362\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Vestre-Coast-Bench-2-810x1203.png\" alt=\"bench detail\" width=\"810\" height=\"1203\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Vestre-Coast-Bench-2-810x1203.png 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Vestre-Coast-Bench-2-800x1188.png 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Vestre-Coast-Bench-2-768x1141.png 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Vestre-Coast-Bench-2-1034x1536.png 1034w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Vestre-Coast-Bench-2.png 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p>Look closely and you&#8217;ll notice marine elements running throughout Coast&#8217;s design: the contours of the front mimic the hull of a boat and the plastic parts give the impression of floating on the surface. The base is made of hot-dip galvanized, powder-coated steel, while the seat is made of recycled plastic. These plastic elements will eventually need to be replaced, so they&#8217;ve been created to do so. They&#8217;ll go back into the recycling pool and be turned into even more new products.</p>\n<p>The initial Coast bench has been produced as a prototype, with toxicity and UV wear tests to come. Vestre&#8217;s goal is to have a limited edition of the bench hit the market in 2021.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=436364\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-436364\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-436364\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Vestre-Coast-Bench-3-810x532.png\" alt=\"bench on beach\" width=\"810\" height=\"532\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Vestre-Coast-Bench-3-810x532.png 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Vestre-Coast-Bench-3-800x525.png 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Vestre-Coast-Bench-3-768x504.png 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Vestre-Coast-Bench-3.png 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=436360\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-436360\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-436360\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Vestre-Coast-Bench-4-810x1206.png\" alt=\"bench detail\" width=\"810\" height=\"1206\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Vestre-Coast-Bench-4-810x1206.png 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Vestre-Coast-Bench-4-800x1191.png 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Vestre-Coast-Bench-4-768x1143.png 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Vestre-Coast-Bench-4-1032x1536.png 1032w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Vestre-Coast-Bench-4.png 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p><a href=\"https://vestre.com/us/news/the-world-s-first-bench-made-from-ownerless-marine-plastic\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Coast</a> is currently in the prototype phase, with plans to release a limited edition in 2021.</p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t<img src=\"http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/design-milk/~4/ymEvHuRRrG0\" height=\"1\" width=\"1\" 16:00:31","updatedTime":"2020-12-11 16:00:31","title":"Laetitia Jacquetton’s Powerful Organic Glass + Rock Forms","link":"https://design-milk.com/?p=436111","description":"\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/laetitia-jacquettons-powerful-organic-glass-rock-forms/lauren-manoogian-laetitia-jacquetton-giant-turtle-featured-image/\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Lauren-Manoogian-Laetitia-Jacquetton-Giant-Turtle-Featured-Image-810x538.jpg\" alt=\"Laetitia Jacquetton&#8217;s Powerful Organic Glass + Rock Forms\" /></a></p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p>After a professional start as designer and maker, Paris-based <a href=\"https://www.instagram.com/laetitiajacquetton/?hl=en\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Lætitia Jacquetton</a> has recently done a deep dive into glass blowing. Her studies took her to Murano, Italy and Eastern France near Nancy to hone her craft. The concept of Jacquetton’s work involves intricately blowing glass around collected rocks to create rare, organic abstract forms.</p>\n<div id=\"attachment_436115\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\"><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=436115\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-436115\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"size-large wp-image-436115\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Lauren-Manoogian-Laetitia-Jacquetton-ALTO-810x1215.jpg\" alt=\"glass vessel and rock\" width=\"810\" height=\"1215\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Lauren-Manoogian-Laetitia-Jacquetton-ALTO-810x1215.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Lauren-Manoogian-Laetitia-Jacquetton-ALTO-800x1200.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Lauren-Manoogian-Laetitia-Jacquetton-ALTO-768x1152.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Lauren-Manoogian-Laetitia-Jacquetton-ALTO-1024x1536.jpg 1024w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Lauren-Manoogian-Laetitia-Jacquetton-ALTO.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a><p class=\"wp-caption-text\">ALTO</p></div>\n<p>It was a trip to a stone garden in Kyoto, Japan that first made Jacquetton think of glass and rock working together. She explains, “Glass blowing is about gravity, it is both intimate and intricate. There is humility involved – too much intention constraining the glass results in a disappointing form. The tension exists moreso between the rock and glass than myself and the glass. I am merely an enabler between the two. And in a way&#8230; it is actually more about the rock than the glass. It is essential to understand the energy of the rock; there is a connection to listen to. Patience and tactile precision are required – the transference of 1000°c glass onto a cold rock can crack it.”</p>\n<div id=\"attachment_436116\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\"><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=436116\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-436116\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"size-large wp-image-436116\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Lauren-Manoogian-Laetitia-Jacquetton-BABY-BUBBLE-WHITE-810x1215.jpg\" alt=\"glass vessel and rock\" width=\"810\" height=\"1215\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Lauren-Manoogian-Laetitia-Jacquetton-BABY-BUBBLE-WHITE-810x1215.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Lauren-Manoogian-Laetitia-Jacquetton-BABY-BUBBLE-WHITE-800x1200.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Lauren-Manoogian-Laetitia-Jacquetton-BABY-BUBBLE-WHITE-768x1152.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Lauren-Manoogian-Laetitia-Jacquetton-BABY-BUBBLE-WHITE-1024x1536.jpg 1024w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Lauren-Manoogian-Laetitia-Jacquetton-BABY-BUBBLE-WHITE.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a><p class=\"wp-caption-text\">BABY BUBBLE WHITE</p></div>\n<p>Brooklyn-based designer <a href=\"https://laurenmanoogian.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Lauren Manoogian</a> and Jacquetton were introduced a few years ago, and are not only connected through their friendship, but also a shared <a href=\"https://shop.design-milk.com/collections/art\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"exclude\">artistic</a> philosophy of sculpture in their respective mediums of textiles and glass.</p>\n<div id=\"attachment_436117\" class=\"wp-caption Screens","link":"https://design-milk.com/?p=436186","description":"\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/a-sag-harbor-hideaway-with-black-slats-creating-privacy-shade-screens/harbor-hideaway-ny-up-studio-1/\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Harbor-Hideaway-NY-Up-Studio-1-810x540.jpg\" alt=\"A Sag Harbor Hideaway With Black Slats Creating Privacy + Shade Screens\" /></a></p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p>Big cities have experienced a record number of people fleeing to more tranquil areas with more square footage and outdoor spaces for an escape from the ongoing pandemic. Seasonal locations have become full-time landing spots, especially as businesses shifted to remote working situations. The small town of Sag Harbor, New York, has become one of those desired locales and this <a href=\"https://www.theupstudio.com/harborhideaway.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">2,630-square-foot residence</a> is the perfect escape. <a href=\"https://www.theupstudio.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">The Up Studio</a> designed the Harbor Hideaway as a single family home on a corner lot with no direct views of the water. Due to its location on a wide street corner they flipped the home&#8217;s orientation so it faced the rear corner of the backyard allowing for privacy and an open flow to the outdoor space.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=436188\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-436188\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-436188\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Harbor-Hideaway-NY-Up-Studio-2-810x540.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"540\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Harbor-Hideaway-NY-Up-Studio-2-810x540.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Harbor-Hideaway-NY-Up-Studio-2-800x533.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Harbor-Hideaway-NY-Up-Studio-2-768x512.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Harbor-Hideaway-NY-Up-Studio-2.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=436189\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-436189\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-436189\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Harbor-Hideaway-NY-Up-Studio-3-810x1013.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"1013\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Harbor-Hideaway-NY-Up-Studio-3-810x1013.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Harbor-Hideaway-NY-Up-Studio-3-800x1000.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Harbor-Hideaway-NY-Up-Studio-3-768x960.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Harbor-Hideaway-NY-Up-Studio-3-1229x1536.jpg 1229w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Harbor-Hideaway-NY-Up-Studio-3.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p>In addition to the black cedar slats that wrap the structure, floor-to-ceiling, black framed windows on the back add additional visual appeal with bold vertical lines. The Up Studio partnered with <a href=\"https://www.marvin.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Marvin Windows</a>, who made custom Marvin Modern windows for the project, which resulted in the back of the home being fully glazed, allowing the morning sun to light up the bedrooms.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=436190\" https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Harbor-Hideaway-NY-Up-Studio-4.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=436191\" Swallow","link":"https://design-milk.com/?p=435690","description":"\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/koskas-capsule-collection-offers-an-easy-pill-to-swallow/koska_cai_4773_300dpi/\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/11/Koska_CAI_4773_300dpi-810x622.jpg\" alt=\"KOSKA&#8217;s Capsule Collection Offers an Easy Pill To Swallow\" /></a></p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p>Founded by Mickaël Koska, the eponymous <a href=\"https://www.mickaelkoska.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">KOSKA</a>, a Marseille-based studio specializes in home furnishings and accessories ranging from mirrors to tables to wall hooks. The studio&#8217;s playful collection of capsule-like lighting and cacti-shaped lamps feature LED filament bulbs that are evocative of the designer&#8217;s childhood.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=435692\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-435692\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-435692\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/11/Koska_CAI_4746_300dpi75-810x682.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"682\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/11/Koska_CAI_4746_300dpi75-810x682.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/11/Koska_CAI_4746_300dpi75-800x673.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/11/Koska_CAI_4746_300dpi75-768x646.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/11/Koska_CAI_4746_300dpi75.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p>If the Coco looks like an egg, it&#8217;s no mistake – the powder coated steel lamp was inspired by the designer&#8217;s childhood memories of an egg cup. The Coco is available in a multitude of finishes, spanning from <a href=\"https://www.mickaelkoska.com/lights/coco-moutarde\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">colorful</a> to <a href=\"https://www.mickaelkoska.com/lights/coco-gold\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">luxe</a> with a few options finished with an <a href=\"https://www.mickaelkoska.com/lights/coco-beton-chataigne\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">earthly patina</a>.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=435693\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-435693\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-435693\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/11/Koska_CAI_4712_300dpi-810x654.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"654\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/11/Koska_CAI_4712_300dpi-810x654.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/11/Koska_CAI_4712_300dpi-800x646.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/11/Koska_CAI_4712_300dpi-768x620.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/11/Koska_CAI_4712_300dpi.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p>Each handmade lamp features an old school style LED filament globe light bulb nested into a steel or wooden base, resulting in a singular capsule form intended to produce a warm secondary light source for surfaces or in larger editions, on the floor.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=435694\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-435694\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-435694\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/11/Koska_CAI_4712_300dpi-1-810x715.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"715\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/11/Koska_CAI_4712_300dpi-1-810x715.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/11/Koska_CAI_4712_300dpi-1-800x706.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/11/Koska_CAI_4712_300dpi-1-768x678.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/11/Koska_CAI_4712_300dpi-1.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p>KOSKA expands on the idea – literally – with the <a href=\"https://www.mickaelkoska.com/lights/cactus-3-tubes\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Cactus tube floor lamps</a>, a linear abstraction of the desert plant finished in borosilicate glass, paired with vertical LED tube lighting and terracotta bases, or adorned with aluminum bands.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=435744\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-435744\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-435744\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/11/Koska-cactus-ambient-810x810.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"810\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/11/Koska-cactus-ambient-810x810.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/11/Koska-cactus-ambient-800x800.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/11/Koska-cactus-ambient-100x100.jpg 100w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/11/Koska-cactus-ambient-768x768.jpg 768w, 16:00:31","updatedTime":"2020-12-11 16:00:31","title":"Gift Unique and Unexpected Chocolates by London-Based BRIK","link":"https://design-milk.com/?p=436272","description":"\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/gift-unique-and-unexpected-chocolates-by-london-based-brik/pinch-taste-brik-chocolate-1-andy_barter/\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Pinch-Taste-BRIK-chocolate-1-Andy_Barter-810x608.jpg\" alt=\"Gift Unique and Unexpected Chocolates by London-Based BRIK\" /></a></p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p>For those who cannot be with their loved ones over the up-and-coming holiday meals… consider sending some truly unique and unexpected sweets that strike conversation and intrigue.</p>\n<p>London-based chocolate company <a href=\"https://brik.site/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">BRIK</a> is breaking the mold with its approach to chocolate. Headed by Danish designer Kia Utzon-Frank (great niece of Sydney Opera House architect Jørn Utzon) and retail strategist Raffaella Baruzzo, BRIK uses textures, materials and architectural surfaces as inspiration for its creations and as a vehicle for amazing flavor combinations.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=436277\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-436277\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-436277\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Pinch-Taste-BRIK-chocolate-2-Domes-810x1491.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"1491\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Pinch-Taste-BRIK-chocolate-2-Domes-810x1491.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Pinch-Taste-BRIK-chocolate-2-Domes-800x1473.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Pinch-Taste-BRIK-chocolate-2-Domes-768x1414.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Pinch-Taste-BRIK-chocolate-2-Domes-834x1536.jpg 834w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Pinch-Taste-BRIK-chocolate-2-Domes-1113x2048.jpg 1113w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Pinch-Taste-BRIK-chocolate-2-Domes.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p>The chocolate tastes as intriguing as it looks and is created using only natural ingredients, plastic free packaging and produced in the most sustainable way possible.</p>\n<p>Kia Utzon-Frank comments: “We are constantly playing with the ambiguity of edible vs non-edible, the inspiration from the natural and industrial worlds. We want to catch people&#8217;s unawares and spark a reaction of curiosity, of amazement, and of surprise, resulting in having them look at our chocolate in the same way they’d look at an awe-inspiring building or a technological wonder.”</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=436278\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-436278\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-436278\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Pinch-Taste-BRIK-chocolate-3-810x456.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"456\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Pinch-Taste-BRIK-chocolate-3-810x456.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Pinch-Taste-BRIK-chocolate-3-800x450.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Pinch-Taste-BRIK-chocolate-3-768x432.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Pinch-Taste-BRIK-chocolate-3-600x337.jpg 600w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Pinch-Taste-BRIK-chocolate-3.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p>From slabs to spheres, the chocolate comes in a variety of sizes and shapes all overseen by Kia over the course of several days. Each and every piece is unique, as there is no set-in-stone technique.</p>\n<p>As well as experimenting with size and shape, they aim to appeal to all five taste receptors: sweet, sour, bitter, salty and umami. They use all natural ingredients sourced with great care, organic bergamot from Calabria, organic South European rosemary with notes of lemon, high grade matcha harvested by a family business in Kyoto, vegan chocolate bases supplied by botanists and activated charcoal from burnt coconut.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=436279\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-436279\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-436279\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Pinch-Taste-BRIK-chocolate-4-Charred-wood-810x992.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"992\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Pinch-Taste-BRIK-chocolate-4-Charred-wood-810x992.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Pinch-Taste-BRIK-chocolate-4-Charred-wood-800x980.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Pinch-Taste-BRIK-chocolate-4-Charred-wood-768x941.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Pinch-Taste-BRIK-chocolate-4-Charred-wood-1254x1536.jpg 1254w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/12/Pinch-Taste-BRIK-chocolate-4-Charred-wood.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p>BRIK also cares deeply about the planet; every aspect of the company, from naturally sourced ingredients to plastic-free compostable packaging, aims to be as sustainable as possible for a small company.</p>\n<p>Raffaella explains: “For us, sustainability is not an option – it’s a given. We use only natural ingredients and have very little waste production. We also work with local charities on enhancing knowledge of food and health for children, as well as global tree planting charities. A percentage of our profit goes towards this work and all employees are encouraged to volunteer.”</p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t<img src=\"http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/design-milk/~4/GXdkQpkPcBU\" /></a></p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p>Following the lines of <a href=\"https://design-milk.com/pantone-color-year-2016-serenity-rose-quartz/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\">2016</a>, <a href=\"https://www.pantone.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Pantone</a> has chosen two colors for the Pantone Color of the Year 2021: <strong>PANTONE 17-5104 Ultimate Gray</strong> and <strong>PANTONE 13-0647 Illuminating</strong>. After the turmoil of 2020, the global color authority selected two contrasting colors that join forces to support and complement each other. Ultimate Gray is fairly neutral evoking feelings of dependability and resilience, while Illuminating is a cheery yellow that&#8217;s bright and sunny with an overall optimistic feel. Brought together, the color pairing offers hope and stability.</p>\n<p>“The Pantone Color of the Year reflects what is taking place in our global culture, expressing what people are looking for that color can hope to answer,&#8221; says Laurie Pressman, Vice President of the Pantone Color Institute. “As society continues to recognize color as a critical form of communication, and a way to symbolize thoughts and ideas, many designers and brands are embracing the language of color to engage and connect.”</p>\n<p>Take a look back at previous Pantone Color of the Year picks <a href=\"https://design-milk.com/tag/pantone-color-of-the-year/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\">here</a>!</p>\n<p>Does the color combination inspire you to bring some of it into your own life and home?
